                     <itype>1</itype>        
                     <orth lang="ar">عَقڤلَ</orth>
                  </form> [The inf. n.] <foreign lang="ar">عَقْلٌ</foreign> signifies The act of <hi rend="ital">withholding,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">restraining;</hi> syn. <foreign lang="ar">مَنْعٌ</foreign>. (TA.) [This is app. the primary signification, or it may be from what next follows.]          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">عَقَلَ البَعِيرَ</foreign>, (S, Mgh, O, Msb, K,) aor.      
    <form n="infl">       
                     <orth orig="Bi" lang="ar">عَقِلَ</orth>
                  </form>, (S, O, Msb,) inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">عَقْلٌ</foreign>, (S, Mgh, O, Msb,) <hi rend="ital">He bound the camel with the</hi> [<hi rend="ital">rope called</hi>] <foreign lang="ar">عِقَال</foreign>; (Mgh;) meaning <hi rend="ital">he bound the camel's fore shank to his arm;</hi> (K;) i. e. <hi rend="ital">he folded together the camel's fore shank and his arm and bound them both in the middle of the arm with the rope called</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">عِقَال</foreign>; (S, O, Msb;) and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n29976-0-1" target="اعتقلهُ" n="1" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign> signifies the same; as also   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n29976-0-2" target="عقّلهُ" n="2" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n29976-0"/></foreign>; (K;) or you say, <foreign lang="ar">عَقَّلْتُ الإِبِلَ</foreign>, from <foreign lang="ar">العِقَالُ</foreign>, (S, O,) inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">تَعْقِيلٌ</foreign>, (O,) [i. e. <hi rend="ital">I bound the camels in the manner expl. above,</hi>] this verb being with tesh-deed because of its application to a number of objects: (S, O:) and sometimes the hocks were bound with the <foreign lang="ar">عِقَال</foreign>. (TA.) The she-camel, also, was bound with the <foreign lang="ar">عِقَال</foreign> on the occasion of her being covered:          <sense type="b" n="3">-b3-</sense>  and hence <foreign lang="ar">العَقْلُ</foreign> is metonymically used as meaning <foreign lang="ar">الجِمَاعُ</foreign> [i. e. <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  <hi rend="ital">The act of compressing</hi> a woman]. (TA.)          <sense type="b" n="4">-b4-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">عَقَلْتُ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">القَتِيلَ</foreign>, (S, Mgh, Msb, K, *) or <foreign lang="ar">المَقْتُولَ</foreign>, (S, O,) aor. as above, (TA,) and so the inf. n., (Msb, TA,) means <hi rend="ital">I gave,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">paid, the bloodwit to the heir,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">next of kin, of the slain person:</hi> (S, Mgh, O, Msb, K: *) for the camels [that constituted the bloodwit] used to be bound with the <foreign lang="ar">عِقَال</foreign> in the yard of the abode of the heir, or next of kin, of the slain person; and in consequence of frequency of usage, the phrase became employed to mean thus when the bloodwit was given in dirhems or deenárs. (As, S, O, Msb. * [See a verse cited in the first paragraph of art. <foreign lang="ar">عيف</foreign>.]) And [hence] one says also, <foreign lang="ar">عَقَلْتُ عَنْهُ</foreign>, (inf. n. as above, TA,) meaning <hi rend="ital">I paid for him,</hi> (the slayer, Mgh,) i. e., <hi rend="ital">in his stead,</hi> (S, Mgh, O, Msb, K, *) <hi rend="ital">the bloodwit that was obligatory upon him,</hi> (S, Mgh, O, K, *) or <hi rend="ital">what was obligatory upon him of the bloodwit.</hi> (Msb.) And <foreign lang="ar">عَقَلْتُ لَهُ دَمَ فُلَانٍ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">I relinquished in his favour retaliation of the blood of such a one for the bloodwit.</hi> (S, O, Msb, K. *) <foreign lang="ar">لَا تَعْقِلُ العَاقِلَةُ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">عَمْدًا وَلَا عَبْدًا</foreign>, (S, Mgh, O, Msb, K,) in a trad. (S, O, Msb) of Esh-Shaabee, (O,) or a saying of Esh-Shaabee, (Mgh, * K,) not a trad., (K,) but the like occurs in a trad. related on the authority of I'Ab, (TA,) [meaning, accord. to an expl. of the verb when trans. without a particle, mentioned above, <hi rend="ital">Those who are responsible for the payment of a bloodwit</hi> in certain cases <hi rend="ital">shall not pay it for an intentional act</hi> of slaying or the like, <hi rend="ital">nor for</hi> the slaying or the like of <hi rend="ital">a slave,</hi>] applies, accord. to Aboo-Haneefeh, to the case of a slave's committing a crime against a free person: (S, O, Msb, K: [and thus as expl. in the Mgh:]) but, (S, O, Msb, K,) accord. to Ibn-Abee-Leylà, (S, O, Msb,) it applies to the case of a free person's committing a crime against a slave; for if the meaning were as Aboo-Haneefeh says, the phrase would be <foreign lang="ar">لَا تَعْقِلُ العَاقِلَةُ عَنْ عَبْدٍ</foreign>; (S, O, Msb, K;) and As pronounced this to be correct: (S, O, Msb: *) Akmal-ed-Deen, however, in the Exposition of the Hidáyeh, says that <foreign lang="ar">عَقَلْتُهُ</foreign> is used in the sense of <foreign lang="ar">عَقَلْتُ عَنْهُ</foreign>, and that the context of the trad. indicates this meaning, which MF also defends. (TA.) [See also the saying <foreign lang="ar">لَا أَعْقِلُ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">الكَلْبَ الهَرَّارَ</foreign> in art. <foreign lang="ar">هر</foreign>.]          <sense type="b" n="5">-b5-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">عَقَلَهُ</foreign>, inf. n. as above, also means <hi rend="ital">He set him up</hi> [app. a man] <hi rend="ital">on one of his legs;</hi> [app. from <foreign lang="ar">عَقَلَ البَعِيرَ</foreign>;] as also <foreign lang="ar">عَكَلَهُ</foreign>: and every <foreign lang="ar">عَقْل</foreign> is <hi rend="ital">a raising.</hi> (TA.)          <sense type="b" n="6">-b6-</sense>  Also, [agreeably with the explanation of the inf. n. in the first sentence of this art.,] and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n29976-0-3" target="عقّلهُ" n="3" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n29976-0"/></foreign>, and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n29976-0-4" target="تعقّلهُ" n="4" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n29979"/></foreign>, (TA, [see also the first paragraph of art. <foreign lang="ar">عجس</foreign>,]) and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n29976-0-5" target="اعتقلهُ" n="5" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign>, (Msb, TA,) <hi rend="ital">He withheld him,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">restrained him,</hi> (Msb, TA,) <foreign lang="ar">عَنْ حَاجَتِهِ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">from the object of his want.</hi> (TA.)          <sense type="b" n="7">-b7-</sense>  And [hence,] <foreign lang="ar">عَقَلَ الدَّوَآءُ بَطْنَهُ</foreign>, (S, O, Msb, K,) aor.

                     <orth orig="Bi" lang="ar">عَقِلَ</orth>
                  </form> (S, K) and

                  </form>, (K,) inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">عَقْلٌ</foreign>, (TA,) <hi rend="ital">The medicine bound,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">confined, his belly</hi> [or <hi rend="ital">bowels</hi>]; syn. <foreign lang="ar">أَمْسَكَهُ</foreign>: (S, O, Msb, K:) accord. to some, particularly <hi rend="ital">after looseness:</hi> and <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n29976-0-6" target="اعتقل" n="6" type="5" subtype="FSO" lang="ar"/>بَطْنَهُ</foreign> signifies the same. (TA.)          <sense type="b" n="8">-b8-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">عَقَلَ عَلَى القَوْمِ</foreign>, [aor.      
    <form n="infl">       
                     <orth orig="Bi" lang="ar">عَقِلَ</orth>
                  </form>,] inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">عِقَالٌ</foreign>, means <hi rend="ital">He collected,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">exacted, the poor-rates of the people,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">party;</hi> [app. from <foreign lang="ar">عَقَلَ البَعِيرَ</foreign>; as though he bound with the rope called <foreign lang="ar">عِقَال</foreign> the camels that he collected;] on the authority of IKtt.       <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n29991-1" target="عَاقِلَةٌ" n="1" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n29992"/></foreign>: (Msb:) the latter is an epithet in which the quality of a subst. predominates; (TA;) and signifies a man's <hi rend="ital">party</hi> (S, Mgh, O, K, TA) <hi rend="ital">who league together to defend one another,</hi> (S, O, K, TA,) <hi rend="ital">consisting of the relations on the father's side,</hi> (S, Mgh, * O, TA,) <hi rend="ital">who pay the bloodwit</hi> (S, Mgh, O, TA) [app. <hi rend="ital">in conjunction with the slayer</hi>] <hi rend="ital">for him who has been slain unintentionally:</hi> (S, O, TA:) it was decided by the Prophet that it was to be paid in three years, to the heirs of the person slain: (TA:) they look to the offender's brothers on the father's side, who, if they take it upon them, pay it in three years: if they do not take it upon them, the debt is transferred to the sons [meaning all the male descendants] of his grandfather; and in default of their doing so, to those of his father's grandfather; and in default of their doing so, to those of his grandfather's grandfather; and so on: it is not transferred from any one of these classes unless they are unable [to pay it]: and such as are enrolled in a register [of soldiers or pensioners or any corporation] are alike in respect of the bloodwit: (IAth, TA:) or, accord. to the people of El-'Irák, it means the <hi rend="ital">persons enrolled in the registers</hi> [<hi rend="ital">of soldiers</hi> or <hi rend="ital">of others</hi>]: (S, O:) or it is applied to the <hi rend="ital">persons of the register which was that of the slayer; but that they bear responsibility [only] in proportion to their ability; and that if there is no <foreign lang="ar">عَاقِلَة</foreign>, it [i. e. the bloodwit] is not to be from the property of the offender; but Is-hák says that in this case it is to be from the treasury of the state, the bloodwit not being [in any case] made a thing of no account: (TA:) the pl. of <foreign lang="ar">عَاقِلَةٌ</foreign> thus applied is <foreign lang="ar">عَوَاقِلُ</foreign>.                   <hi rend="ital">A place to which one betakes himself for refuge, protection, preservation, covert,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">lodging;</hi> syn. <foreign lang="ar">مَلْجَأٌ</foreign>; (S, Mgh, O, Msb, K;) as also

(TA.)
